SR's financial administration expenditure on the management of excise duties is steadily increasing, as, with the exception of wage growth, investments for efficient tax administration and the electronisation of financial administration are increasing.
Although excise revenues increased, spending grew faster as a result of IT adjustments related to the UNITAS project.
Wage expenditure in the Czech Republic is significantly affected by the performance of permanent tax supervision in tax warehouses for alcohol, which is not applied by the Czech Republic.
Expenditure of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic on the administration of excise duties increased more significantly between 2012 and 2015, this growth was mainly due to the increase in wage and technical support expenditure.
In the Czech Republic, revenues from excise duties also grew at approximately the same rate.
Wage expenditure in the Czech Republic is positively influenced by the wider competences of the customs administration compared to the Czech Republic, e.g. weighing of trucks, control of compliance with obligations in connection with the toll.
The efficiency of administrative costs in the SR shows a slightly deteriorating trend year-on-year.
The number of employees did not change significantly, but the expenditure per employee increased.
Also in the Czech Republic, the number of employees did not change significantly, but expenditure per employee increased more slowly compared to the SR.
Evaluation
In the Czech Republic and the Czech Republic, wage growth is a significant factor in the deterioration of the efficiency of administrative expenditure, which can be evaluated as a natural development.
In both countries, maintaining significant administrative burdens in the management of excise duties appears to be a negative factor, which is confirmed by the non-decreasing number of employees in the field of excise duty management.
In The Czech Technical League, however, the management of excise duties at lower incomes is significantly more demanding on personnel capacities.
Performance indicators for the administration of excise duties
Excise management is a set of activities that aim to correctly identify, determine, and secure the payment of tax.
The main processes in the management of excise duties are the assessment of taxes, authorisation and registration for activities, supervision of transport, control and search of tax entities.
The number of administrative tasks and managed entities are indicators of the performance of the tax administrator.
The correlation between the monitored indicator and the number of tax authorities expresses the effectiveness of the tax administrator's activities and defines the cost of a particular activity.
Authorisation and registration are a prerequisite for the handling and transport of selected products for commercial purposes under the suspensive exemption regime.
The tax administrator is obliged to carry out continuous administration with the authorisation or registration entities with a focus on supervising compliance with the legislation and conditions laid down by the tax administrator, for which adequate personnel resources must be allocated.
The monitored indicator was the number of valid authorisations or registrations to operate as at 31 December 2004. 1.
The number of authorisations or registrations issued is not the same as the number of tax entities.
Administrative acts are specific administrative acts in the case.
The administrative tasks pursued are the frequency of the most important acts of the tax administrator (tax claim, administration of transport in EMCS), or activities which are a sequence of acts terminated by a report or decision.
Performance indicators in the Czech Republic
Authorisation and registration to operate in the Czech Republic
Tax warehouse:
You can produce, process, store, receive, or ship selected products by permission of the tax administrator to run the tax warehouse.
If the tax warehouse operator has more than one warehouse, a permit shall be issued for each separately, including tax security.
Tax security is not required in the case of distilleries under the permanent tax supervision of the tax administrator (i.e. the physical presence of the official and the provision of equipment by the conclusion of the tax administrator).
In the Czech Republic, permanent tax supervision is not applied.
The operator of the tax warehouse also registers for tax pursuant to Section 125 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.
An authorisation to operate a tax warehouse is a condition for the transport of selected products conditionally exempt from the place of importation to the tax warehouse, to the authorised consignee in another Member State, to the place of export in another Member State or to a consignee in another Member State (replaces the status of registered consignor in accordance with Article 4(10) of Council Directive 2008/118/EC).
Tax warehouse statistics do not include permits for the acquisition of electricity, natural gas and solid fuels tax-free, which are analogous to the authorisation of a tax warehouse.
The distillery produces alcohol with a reduced 50% tax rate (CZK 14,300/hl ethanol) – fruit spirits for growers. It is not a tax warehouse and the permit to operate is issued by the Ministry of Agriculture.
The reduced tax rate can be applied to 30 litres of pure alcohol per household of a grower intended for personal consumption for the production period (July-June).
The records of the distillation produced by the operators of the distillery and made available to the tax authorities shall contain information on the grower, the basic raw material, the distillate issued, the origin of the fruit and the production of the distillate.
The beneficiary for the re-reception of the selected products and the beneficiary for the single admission of the selected products shall be entitled, on a one-off basis, to accept or re-receive the selected products in a conditional system transported from another Member State on a one-off basis.
The beneficiary is not the operator of the tax warehouse and may not store or ship the selected products under the suspensive exemption scheme.
The user of selected exempt products is a legal or natural person who receives and uses, or pursuant to § 52a or § 53 of Act No. 353/2003 Coll. sells to another user selected exempt products; users have the status of tax entities without the obligation to register for tax.
The exempted products selected may be accepted and used only on the basis of a final authorisation, and only from the supplier specified in the authorisation.
On the basis of an authorisation, exempt mineral oils may be sold to another holder of the authorisation or to a user who is authorised to use mineral oils without authorisation.
Mineral oils exempt ed may be sold without authorisation in statutory cases, e.g.:
waste oils in quantities of less than 10 000 litres per calendar year, if the user has produced or originated in his or her activities,
collected tax-exempt mineral oils in a unit packet of not more than 20 litres intended for purposes other than engine propulsion or heat production, and at the same time intended for sale to the final consumer.
Selected exempt products may be transported with proof of exemption.
The distributor of spirits in consumer packaging is entitled to sell or otherwise transfer the alcohol indicated for free circulation after compulsory registration with the tax administrator.
The raw tobacco storer is entitled, on the basis of registration with the tax authorities and the conditions laid down, to store raw tobacco for a purpose other than the manufacture of tobacco products.
A person loading special mineral oils shall be entitled, on the basis of registration with the tax authorities and the conditions laid down, to acquire, sell or otherwise transfer special mineral oils which are bulk or placed in packages exceeding 220 litres.
The fuel distributor is entitled to sell fuel in the Czech Republic, with the exception of the sale of fuel from a petrol station, on the basis of the issued concession and the registration of the tax administrator under specified conditions.
Phm transport must be accompanied by a tax document, proof of sale or proof of transport, or delivery plan and bottling tickets.
These documents may be replaced by electronic documents sent before the start of transport to the tax authorities.
The service station operator owns fuel sold at the service station.
Gas stations are places where, on the basis of the permission of the building authority, the sale or dispensing of PHM is usually allowed into the fuel tank.
The Ministry of Industry and Trade registers service stations and their operators broken down into: registered – normal sale or issue of PHM, as a rule, in the fuel tanks of vehicles; with a defined approach – operation usually in various business premises (e.g. quarries, sawmills, farms, transport organizations, building yards), the sale is carried out here limited to the other party on the basis of specific contractual relations; non-public – fuel dispensing points only for the operators' own consumption.
The pumping station is not a construction or equipment in the form of an operating tank placed in operation (e.g. on a chassis) if the fuel is issued only for its own use.
Operating tanks are not subject to the tax authorities' permission and are not registered.
Natural and legal persons may purchase, receive and sell liquefied petroleum gases placed for free circulation for resale by natural and legal persons under the authorisation of the tax administrator.
They shall also be authorised where they purchase or obtain liquefied petroleum gas for their own consumption exceeding 20 tonnes per calendar year.
Administrative tasks in the Czech Republic
Tax control is a set of actions. Tax control shall be subject to tax obligations, claims by the tax entity or other circumstances relevant to the correct determination and determination of the tax relating to one tax procedure.
Tax control can be carried out jointly for multiple tax proceedings of a single tax entity.
Repeated tax control can only be carried out under the conditions laid down by law and justifications when the inspection is initiated.
Tax control is carried out within the period for determining the tax, which is three years, the period being extended by one year under the conditions laid down by law (e.g. filing additional tax proceedings, initiating criminal proceedings in connection with the tax in question), or being opposed (judicial proceedings, international cooperation).
The time limit for determining the tax shall end no later than the expiry of 10 years from the expiry of the period for making a proper tax claim.
The tax authorities are not obliged to carry out a tax audit on each tax entity.
The start of the tax audit puts up time limits for the possibility of submitting an additional tax return or additional billing by the tax entity (Section 141 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.) and restarts the period for determining the tax (Section 148 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.).
On the basis of its outcome, the ex officio tax may be adjusted.
A local investigation is an individual time-bound action (one day) in which the tax administrator searches for evidence and conducts examinations of premises, goods, documents, records, means of transport and transport packages for tax entities and other persons involved in tax administration, on the spot outside the premises of the tax administrator (e.g. at the tax entity, at the point of sale, on the road during transport).
The tax administrator is entitled to borrow documents and belongings, take samples or arrange them.
Based on the outcome of the local investigation, the tax cannot be individually adjusted, but the tax entity can be asked to file an additional tax return (Section 145(2) of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.).
The control of transport data in the EMCS is not a local investigation.
The order of the alcohol marking checklists may only be placed by the registered person obliged to mark the alcohol to the tax authorities and is made by means of smart forms, which are automatically imported into the application of the spirit label register.
The tax administrator processes the order, evaluates the adequacy of the ordered quantity of check strips, and orders production.
He does not supervise the production of control tapes.
Production is provided by the State Printing House of Valuables, a state-owned enterprise.
The customer of the control tapes takes control tapes from the tax administrator at the local place of the marking point.
Ordering tobacco stickers to label cigarettes, cigarillos, cigars and tobacco for smoking acts as a tax return.
The value of the tobacco sticker corresponds to the amount of the tax liability, and the purchaser of tobacco stickers is obliged to pay their value within 60 days from the date of their removal from the tax authorities.
The customer is obliged to calculate in the order the value corresponding to the amount of tax liability of the ordered tobacco stickers.
This period applies only if the value of the tobacco stickers is ensured.
An order for tobacco stickers is placed on a form provided by the Ministry of Finance in writing or via a data box with the possibility of using smart forms.
The production of tobacco stickers is provided by the State Printing House of Cenin, a state-owned company.
The authorized tax administrator, which is the Customs Office for the Central Bohemian Region (territorial office Kutná Hora), ensures the purchase and transport of tobacco stickers to the tax administrator, who redistributes them and further verifies their transport, storage and use of them at customers.
Tax claims include proper tax returns, additional and corrective tax returns, including orders for tobacco stickers, filed by tax entities.
The customs declaration of vat shall not be included on the basis of customs declarations and the declaration of recovery of refund rights from: mineral oils used for the production of heat, other petrol used in the course of business activities other than for the production of heat or the propulsion of engines, mineral oils used for agricultural primary production.
The fines imposed include administrative proceedings for the consideration of infringements found, a set of successive administrative acts. The international exchange of information on tax entities (ELO) within the meaning of Council Regulation (EU) No 389/2012 takes the form of: requests for administrative cooperation, replies to a request for administrative cooperation, spontaneous information, event reports, control reports.
Transport under the conditional exemption procedure between the Czech Republic and eu Member States – the Czech customs office is the tax administrator of the receiving or sending tax warehouse or the beneficiary.
Performance indicators in SR
Authorisation and registration to operate in the Czech Air Court
The administration of excise duties in the Czech Technical Association is mainly provided by the customs authorities and the Department of Excise Duties of the Customs and Tax Section of the Czech Technical Office, whose procedure in the administration of excise duties is regulated by the individual excise laws and the tax code.
These laws provide not only the scope of authorisation for the CÚ and the FÚ SR in the administration of excise duties, but also the rights and obligations of tax entities in connection with the registration or payment of excise duty.
The largest year-on-year increase in tax entities (by 234%) was recorded in 2012 and 2013, due to an increase in issued permits within tax warehouses, an increase in the registrations of the beneficiary authorised for the re-recruitment and registration of a large number of user enterprises.
The legislation clarified the transport of certain bulk mineral oils, as well as the notification obligation if they are transported freely or in packages with a content of more than 150 litres and 230 litres respectively, and also extended the list of mineral oils subject to control and transport procedure to include other goods, e.g. mineral oils. o anti-tapping agents, oxidising inhibitors, bituminous inhibitors, viscosity improvement products, anti-corrosion agents.
A mandatory indication has been introduced for lubricating oils concerning the indication of their kinematic viscosity.
The approach of the registration process for selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in the Slovak Technical University is set out in the following sections of the document.
Tax warehouse operator
Within the framework of national legislation of the Slovak System, when registering the tax warehouse operator in the framework of all excise articles, a person who wants to operate a tax warehouse must also apply at the same time for registration and the issue of a permit for the operation of a tax warehouse.
The resulting decision in the registration process is a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty, by which the tax warehouse operator obtains legal personality for all tax warehouses.
At the same time, the CA shall issue an authorisation to operate a tax warehouse which entitles the tax warehouse operator in that tax warehouse to produce, process, store, receive or dispatch selected products under the suspensive exemption scheme.
In the event that the tax warehouse operator has tax warehouses in multiple locations, the tax administrator issues a separate permit for each tax warehouse to operate the tax warehouse.
The transport of the subject of excise duty under the conditional exemption scheme is monitored electronically through the EMCS system.
A unique reference code is generated for each transport, called a reference code.
ARC code under which the said transport can be tracked online and thus in real time.
If the tax warehouse operator is also the person authorised to distribute alcohol, he shall notify the VAT electronically the trade name of the consumer packaging of alcohol, the volume and volume concentration of alcohol in the consumer alcohol packaging and the EAN barcode for each new type of consumer packaging it enters into free tax circulation, no later than the date of its introduction.
Registered sender
The registered consignor is a special type of tax entity which cannot also be registered as a tax warehouse operator at the same time, even if it sends the subject of excise duty under the conditional exemption procedure after its release for free circulation.
Under the national legislation of the Slovak System, when registering a registered consignor in the context of all excise articles, a person who wishes to send the subject of excise duty under the conditional exemption procedure after his placing under the customs procedure 'free circulation', must also apply to the CA for the registration and issue of an authorisation to send the subject of excise duty under that procedure.
The CA shall issue a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty and shall also issue an authorisation to send the subject-matter of excise duty under the suspensive procedure after its entry under the customs procedure 'free circulation'.
Growing distillery
The basic act for the operation of the distillery is to obtain a permit for the production of alcohol in the distillery plant from the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Development of the Czech Republic.
However, the ministry's own authorisation does not entitle the holder of the permit to operate the distillery.
In order for a person to operate a distillery, a person must submit an application to the CA for registration and the issue of a registration certificate for the planting distillery operator.
The CA shall issue a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty, which at the same time entitles the operator of the distillery to produce alcohol in the distillery.
The purpose of the distillery is to provide services to growers.
Grower distillery cannot be a tax warehouse.
The legislature allows for an application of a reduced tax rate of 50 % of the basic rate of tax, i.e. 50 % of the basic rate of tax, to alcohol produced in a distillery. 540 €/hl a.
The reduced rate of tax shall apply to alcohol produced in a distillery in a quantity not exceeding 43 l a. per grower and his household per production period in the tax territory.
The production period shall be as from 1 January 2005. 7. current year to 30 June 2006 6th of the following year.
The production period is not the same as the calendar year and therefore it is possible to apply a reduced tax rate to the alcohol produced several times within a single calendar year because the alcohol is produced in two production periods.
It involves the production of alcohol outside the suspensive exemption scheme, which in practice means that the alcohol produced is in free circulation.
The grower pays not only excise duty and value added tax for the distillery produced, but also the price for the services rendered.
The distillery shall issue the grower a pick-up certificate, which serves not only as proof of the origin and method of acquisition of alcohol, but also of payment of excise duty.
The transport of the alcohol thus produced shall not be subject to monitoring by the tax authorities.
Importer of consumer packaging
National legislation allows persons who intend to import consumer packaging of alcohol or cigarettes from the territory of a third State and to place it in free tax circulation in the tax territory, to apply to the CA for inclusion in the register of importers of consumer packaging.
The importer of consumer packaging does not register with the relevant excise duty, but the CA shall issue it with a certificate of inclusion in the register of importers of consumer packaging.
That certificate authorises importers to import consumer packaging of alcohol or consumer packaging of cigarettes from the territory of a third State.
At the same time, before issuing the control marks, they must lodge a tax guarantee at the rate of the amount of tax attributable to the quantity of alcohol or cigarettes which it wishes to put into free circulation.
Importers of consumer packaging must enter into free tax circulation only consumer packages marked with a check mark.
For this reason, they must submit to the customs office of export the number and identification number of the inspection marks exported to the territory of a third State.
On importation, the importer shall have the number of stamps imported back from the territory of a third State at the customs office of importation.
When importing consumer packaging, the importer proceeds within the meaning of customs legislation, where the amount of excise duty is also included in the customs debt.
In the event of the release of consumer packaging for free circulation, the compound tax guarantee shall be returned to the importer or may be used to pay the customs debt.
The importer of consumer packaging is not a tax stock.
Where the importer of consumer packaging of alcohol is also a person authorised to distribute alcohol, it shall notify the VAT electronically the trade name of the consumer alcohol packaging, the volume and volume concentration of alcohol in the consumer alcohol packaging and the EAN barcode for each new type of consumer packaging it enters into free circulation, no later than the date of its introduction.
Seller of consumer packaging of alcohol in free tax circulation
In order to monitor the movement of alcohol in free tax circulation and to eliminate tax evasion, the legislature introduced a new tax institute for consumer packaging retailers.
A person wishing to hold a permit for sale must apply to the CA for a permit and comply with the legal conditions (commercial authorisation; integrity in relation to intentional economic offences; has not been stripped of a permit for sale for ten years; it is not in liquidation or bankruptcy).
As it is a consumer packaging of alcohol in free circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting such goods.
For example, it is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquiring consumer packaging of alcohol. invoice, which also contains the number of the holder of the distribution authorisation.
The holder of the authorisation shall keep for each establishment in a calendar month a record of the number of consumer packaging of alcohol received, the number of units of consumer packaging of alcohol issued, the stocks of alcohol in consumer alcohol packaging on the last day of the month and the registration of manka or surplus in the number of consumer alcohol packages received and issued.
The holder of the authorisation shall be obliged to purchase or otherwise purchase alcohol in consumer packaging in the course of a business activity only from the person authorised to distribute.
Distributor of consumer packaging alcohol
In order to monitor the movement of alcohol in free tax circulation and eliminate tax evasion, the legislature introduced a new tax institute to distributor consumer packaging of alcohol.
A person who intends to hold a distribution authorisation must apply to the CA for distribution authorisation.
The applicant must comply with the legal conditions (trade licence for trade; storage area exceeds 200 m2; annual turnover from the sale of consumer packaging of alcohol at least €100,000 or paid-up capital of at least €100,000; minimum number of 10 employees; no arrears to the customs office; no arrears on compulsory levies; incomparability in relation to intentional economic crimes; has not been stripped of a sales permit for 10 years; is not in liquidation or bankruptcy).
As it is a consumer packaging of alcohol in free circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting such goods.
It is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of consumer packaging of alcohol e.g. invoice, which also contains the number of the holder of the distribution authorisation.
The holder of the distribution authorisation shall keep for each establishment in a calendar month a record of the number of consumer packaging of alcohol received, the number of units of consumer alcohol packaging issued, the stocks of alcohol in consumer alcohol packaging on the last day of the month and the registration of manka or surplus in the number of consumer alcohol packages received and issued.
The holder of the distribution authorisation is obliged to purchase alcohol in consumer packaging only from another person authorised to distribute.
The person authorised to distribute shall notify the data for each calendar month electronically, by 25 April 2015. the day of the following calendar month.
Fuel dealer
A new type of tax entity, namely the fuel dealer, has been introduced to monitor fuels in free circulation as well as to eliminate tax evasion.
There is no specific regulation governing service stations in the territory of the SR.
Therefore, petrol stations in the national legislation of the Slovak Technical System are incorporated as sellers of fuels.
A person who wishes to sell petrol, diesel or LPG for final consumption in the course of a business activity in the tax territory shall apply to the CA for a sales permit before starting the sale and to provide a document proving that the storage facility is verified and equipped with an appropriate verified measuring device allowing the quantity of mineral oil to be measured at reception and dispensing, and the tank shall comply with the technical standards.
If the fuel vendor is a tax warehouse operator, an authorised consignee or a registered consignor, the CA will also automatically issue a permit for the sale of fuels to registered persons.
The fuel dealer is obliged, among other legal obligations, to keep records of purchased and sold petrol, diesel or LPG in a calendar month and is also obliged to notify the CA of a new supplier (distributor) of fuels.
By law, the fuel dealer is obliged to purchase or otherwise purchase fuels only from a fuel distributor or from a registered person.
As they are fuels in free circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
However, when the fuel is delivered via the car system, the distributor prints the so-called "fuel pumping" to the dealer. from a measuring device built into the car system.
That document shall contain, in addition to the quantities, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the Transport Inspectorate.
It is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellents e.g. invoice, which also contains the fuel distributor number allocated by the tax administrator.
The tax administrator in the territory of the SR records tax evasion related to the transport of this type of goods in the exercise of tax supervision of mineral oils.
Above all, this is an effort to avoid roadside checks during transport, which is why carriers use side roads, bypassing the toll collection system due to more difficult monitoring of actual transports.
Transports of mineral oils in converted double-bottomed tanks are also carried out.
Many times it happens that illegal transport accompanies the vehicle, which carriers report possible mobile patrols in order to change the route and avoid roadside inspection.
The fuels are also mixed with light heating oils or waste oils.
Fuel distributor
A new type of tax entity, namely the fuel distributor, has been introduced to monitor fuels in free circulation as well as to eliminate tax evasion.
A person who intends to distribute petrol, diesel or LPG in the tax territory in the course of a business shall, before starting distribution, apply to the customs office for a distribution permit and produce a document proving that the storage facility is verified and equipped with an appropriate verified measuring equipment, as well as a list of suppliers and customers.
The distributor of fuels is obliged, among other legal obligations, to keep separately for each establishment records of petrol, diesel or LPG sold in a calendar month.
By law, a fuel distributor is obliged to purchase or otherwise purchase fuels only from a fuel distributor or from a registered person.
A fuel distributor may only sell in tax territory to a fuel distributor, registered person or fuel consumer.
However, when the fuel is delivered via the fuel dealer, the distributor prints the so-called "fuel dealer" when pumping the fuel. from a measuring device built into the car system.
That document shall contain, in addition to the quantities, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the Transport Inspectorate.
As they are fuels in free circulation, an accompanying document is not required for the transport of such goods.
It is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellents e.g. invoice, which also contains the number of the fuel distributor or registered person assigned by the tax administrator.
Consumer of fuels
The consumer of propelants has a special position in national legislation.
A person who, in the tax territory, purchases petrol, diesel or LPG for his own consumption in the tax territory and stores this mineral oil in a storage facility of 15 000 litres or more, he shall notify this fact to the customs office no later than the first place in the storage facility.
The consumer of fuels shall be registered by the customs office.
In addition to the legal facts, he is obliged to indicate the address of the storage facility location.
In practice, these are large transport companies, cooperatives, bus companies, road construction companies and other entities.
The storage equipment shall be verified and equipped with a measuring device allowing the quantity of propelling agents (status bar, measuring bar) to be measured at reception and dispensing.
The tank must meet technical standards.
The fuel consumer must purchase fuels only from a fuel distributor or from a registered person.
As they are fuels in free circulation, an accompanying document is not required during transport.
However, when the fuel is delivered via the car cester, the distributor prints the so-called "fuel pumping" to the consumer. from a measuring device built into the car system.
That document shall include, in addition to the information relating to the quantity, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the Transport Inspectorate.
It is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellents e.g. invoice, which also contains the fuel distributor number allocated by the tax administrator.
The tax administrator in the territory of the SR records tax evasion related to the transport of this type of goods in the exercise of tax supervision of mineral oils.
Small independent brewery
The operator of a small independent brewery is a person who produces beer in the course of the business and meets the legal conditions.
Subject to compliance with the statutory conditions, a small independent brewery may apply a reduced tax rate, i.e. a reduced tax rate. € 2,652 per hl/percentage of the actual alcoholic strength.
Annual beer production is limited to the quantity up to 200,000 hl of beer.
As it is the production of beer outside the suspensive exemption regime, there is no need for a accompanying document for transport as it is in free circulation.
A small independent brewery cannot be a tax warehouse.
In practice, they are small family businesses, which also run restaurants or pubs, in which they offer for sale beer of their own production.
Administrative tasks in The Czech
This subchapter approximates the exercise of the tax supervision of the administration of excise duties on selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in the Slovak Technical Party.
The largest year-on-year increase in administrative tasks (by 5.3 %) between 2012 and 2013, which resulted in more EMCS services.
By contrast, the largest decrease was recorded year-on-year in 2014, by up to 4.3%, due to fewer completed tax checks and fewer tax returns filed.
This decrease concerned legislative changes.
Tax controls
By exercising tax control, the CA determines or examines the facts relevant to the correct determination of the tax.
In carrying out tax control, the employees of the CA shall be shown by the mandate to carry out tax control, which includes, inter alia, the purpose and subject-matter of the control and the scope of the tax periods audited.
In practice, this means that the tax year audited can be one month, but also more tax periods.
The scope of the tax periods audited is determined by the CA.
Tax control begins with the registration of the start of the tax audit.
The receipt of the documents will be confirmed by the CA.
The loaned documents are obliged to return the CA within 30 days of the end of the tax audit.
The ca's employee draws up a protocol from the tax audit.
If the tax audit finds a difference in the sum to be paid, declared or claimed by the taxable entity, the CA, together with the protocol audited by the tax entity, shall also send a call for comments on the findings set out in the Protocol.
The tax check is terminated on the date of receipt of the log.
The period for carrying out tax checks shall not exceed one year from the date of its initiating.
Tax control on registered persons and selected registered persons shall be carried out as necessary, but at least once before the date of termination of the right to fix the tax, which is 5 years.
The FŘ SR issued an internal management act adjusting the abovementioned deadlines due to the uniform procedure of the tax administrator in the territory of the SR.
Local investigations
A local inquiry is the activity of a tax administrator in which it seeks evidence, examines and identifies the facts that are needed for tax administration purposes.
A local inquiry is written by an employee of the CA and a copy of it shall be submitted to the tax entity.
In carrying out the local investigation, the ca staff has the right to unrestricted access to land, operating buildings, rooms and places including means of transport, transport containers and accounting documents.
The settlement of the quantity of alcohol produced shall be established in the form of a local investigation.
The facts found are the basis for the exercise of tax control.
Also, in carrying out a local investigation, the CA is entitled to take samples as well as to secure the case.
The FŘ SR issued an internal management act adjusting the performance of tax surveillance and local investigations for individual subjects of excise duties in order to unify the procedures of the tax administrator.
Permanent tax supervision in tax warehouses for alcohol
By the accession of the Slovak Republic to the European Union on 1 January 2005, the Slovak Republic has been a member of the European Union. 5. 2004, there was also a change in the area of excise tax management.
The need for more efficient spending of the state budget in the management of alcohol excise duty, improved the business environment in the area and the introduction of legislative instruments to more effectively suppress the grey economy in the area resulted in the adoption in 2004 of new laws in relation to the administration of excise duties.
One of the measures brought about by the new legislative change was not only the transfer of the tax administrator in the field of the management of excise duties from the tax authorities to customs offices, but also the introduction of the need for the presence of the tax administrator in the tax warehouse on alcohol.
In the territory of the Slovak Republic, the national legislation exhaustively defines that it is possible to receive, issue, produce or process alcohol in a tax warehouse only in the presence of an employee of the CA.
These shall not apply to a tax warehouse which receives, stores or dispatches alcohol only in consumer packaging of alcohol.
At the same time, the CA is obliged to secure employees in the tax warehouse so that the income, supply, production or processing of alcohol is not limited.
The tax warehouse operator is obliged to ensure the conditions of the working environment for the employees of the CA.
On the basis of a contract concluded with FŘ SR for the premises provided on a monthly basis, the CA pays the operator of the tax warehouse the cost of the lease.
In the tax warehouse during the manufacture, processing or storage of alcohol, the production installation for the storage of alcohol must be adapted in such a way that the quantity of alcohol produced, processed alcohol, 100 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 000 0000 000 0
THISsegmentISintentionallyLEFTblank
If alcohol is not accepted, issued, produced or processed in a tax warehouse, the customs office may waive the obligation to ensure the presence of an employee of the customs office, and is obliged to secure this area by closing the customs office.
In practice, however, this option is not used very often because tax warehouse operators use the continuous presence of a customs office employee to their advantage.
Some tax warehouse operators make use of the legal option within the meaning of Act No. 467/2002 Z. z., on the production and marketing of alcohol, and use production facilities for the production of spirits in the distillery for growing burning and also for the purposes of distillate distillate distilleries, which must be a tax warehouse.
Approximately 250 customs officers are provided with permanent tax supervision in alcohol tax warehouses.
Issuing vouchers for the collection of alcohol control marks
The basic act for the collection of control marks is to send an application to the customs office for the allocation of the registration number and the issue of a voucher for the collection of control marks for alcohol.
Alcoholic beverages which are alcohol are goods of combined nomenclatures 2207 and 2208 with an actual alcoholic strength by volume exceeding 1,2 vol.
The control mark is intended for the labelling of consumer packaging of alcohol.
A sealed consumer packaging filled with alcohol intended for direct human consumption is considered to be a consumer packaging of alcohol.
Consumer packaging of the Combined Nomenclature code 2207 and 2208 may be put into free circulation in the tax territory only if it is marked with a control mark.
Only the tax warehouse operator, the authorised consignee and the importer of the consumer packaging who will put it into free circulation may indicate the consumer packaging of alcohol by a control mark.
The check mark contains, inter alia, the identification number consisting of a 14-digit number. The identification number contains the registration number (1-6 instead of the numerical character), the volume of alcohol (7-11 instead of the numeric character) and the volume concentration of alcohol in consumer packaging (12-14 instead of the numeric character).
Original model of the alcohol check mark:
The registration number shall be assigned to each customer by the CA separately.
Only a control mark whose identification number corresponds to the volume of consumer packaging, the volume concentration of alcohol in the consumer packaging and the consumer's control mark may be used to indicate consumer packaging of alcohol.
At the end of 2014, national legislation introduced a new information system for control marks.
The aim of the new control mark information system was to simplify and inform the system of ordering, assessing, printing, distribution and use of control marks intended for the labelling of consumer packaging of alcohol.
Only the tax warehouse operator, the authorised consignee, the consumer packaging importer and the consumer of the alcohol may indicate the consumer packaging with a check mark.
A customer of control marks who wishes to take control marks under the 'new system' must apply to the customs office to issue the control marks electronically.
Through the electronic system, the customer of the control marks is obliged to request their issue, to report the data resulting from the national legislation of the Slovak System and to keep a register of the inspection marks.
The number of pieces of control marks ordered shall not be less than 500 pieces or multiples thereof.
The tax administrator also communicates with the customers of the control marks through the electronic control mark system, in particular when notifying the number of control marks that the customer of the control marks can remove or when determining the date of acceptance of the control marks by the customer of the control marks in the printer.
The customer of the control marks is obliged to deposit funds on behalf of the tax administrator corresponding to the price of the control marks which he may withdraw and the quantity of which shall be notified to him by the customs office before taking control marks.
The price of the check mark takes into account the amount of compensation to the printer. However, it does not take into account the amount of excise duty.
The control stamps are entitled to be printed by the state company Mint Kremnice.
FŘ SR supervises the tax supervision of the handling of control marks and their disposal in the printer.
FŘ SR is obliged to ensure the presence of an employee of the Financial Directorate in the printer when handling the inspection marks.
FŘ SR ensures the sale of control marks to the customer of the inspection marks in the printer.
It is only possible to remove the check marks in the printer from the employee of the Financial Directorate.
Issuing vouchers for the collection of control marks on tobacco products
The customer of the control mark must apply to the CA for the allocation of the registration number and the issue of a voucher for the collection of the control mark.
Consumer packaging of cigarettes can only be put into free circulation if it is marked with a check mark.
It is only possible to label consumer packaging of cigarettes with a check mark in a company that makes cigarettes.
Only the customer of the control marks may be the tax warehouse operator, the authorised consignee or importer of tobacco products who wishes to place tobacco products for free circulation in the tax territory.
Only a control mark whose particulars correspond to the relevant price of cigarettes, the number of cigarettes in the pack, the length of the cigarettes, the expiry date of the tax rate and the registration number may be used to indicate the consumer packaging of cigarettes.
Consumer packaging of cigarettes can only be sold for final consumption at the price indicated on the control mark.
At the end of 2014, national legislation introduced a new information system for control marks.
The aim of the new stamp information system was to simplify and inform the system of ordering, assessing, printing, distribution and use of control marks intended for the labelling of consumer packaging of tobacco, cigars, cigarillos and cigarettes.
A customer of control marks who wishes to take control marks under the 'new system' must apply to the customs office to issue the control marks electronically.
Through the electronic system, the customer of the control marks is obliged to request their issue, to report the data resulting from the national legislation of the Slovak System and to keep a register of the inspection marks.
The control stamps are entitled to be printed by the state company Mint Kremnice.
FŘ SR supervises the tax supervision of the handling of control marks and their disposal in the printer.
FŘ SR is obliged to ensure the presence of an employee of the Financial Directorate in the printer when handling the inspection marks.
FŘ SR ensures the sale of control marks to the customer of the inspection marks in the printer.
It is only possible to remove the check marks in the printer from the employee of the Financial Directorate.
The tax warehouse operator or importer of tobacco products may mark consumer tobacco packaging with a check mark.
The tax warehouse operator, importer of tobacco products or authorised consignee may indicate consumer packaging of cigars or cigarillos with a check mark.
Only a control mark whose particulars correspond to the stamp for the validity of the excise duty rate shall be used to indicate consumer packaging of tobacco, cigars or cigarillos.
It is only possible to label consumer packaging of cigarettes with a check mark in the company that made them.
The number of pieces of control marks ordered shall not be less than 500 pieces or multiples thereof.
The CA shall, within three working days, electronically notify the customer of the control marks the number of inspection marks which they can withdraw, the price of the inspection marks and the account number of the FŘ SR.
A CA may reduce the number of pieces of control marks ordered if there are circumstances on the basis of which it can reasonably be assumed that a tax infringement may occur.
FŘ SR will determine the date of receipt of the inspection marks by the customer of the control marks, but no later than 10 days.
The date of acceptance of the inspection marks of the FŘ SR shall be notified by means of an electronic system of control marks to the customer of the control marks.
The control marks shall be issued by the Financial Directorate exclusively in the printing works, but only after receipt of the funds corresponding to their price to the relevant account specified in the electronic notification of the customs office.
The customer of the control marks is obliged separately in the breakdown for cigarettes, cigars, cigarillos and tobacco to keep a record of the control marks in the electronic control mark system.
Administrative cooperation between EU Member States (ELO)
Within the meaning of Council Regulation (EU) No 389/2012, the ELO and SPD systems of the Department of Excise Duty of the FŘ SR shall be responsible for ensuring the exchange of information upon request for administrative cooperation between EU Member States and the competent financial authorities.
These include, in particular, requests for verification of entities in the context of excise duty management, requests for information relating to the administration of excise duties, as well as requests for confirmation of information from the SEED database.
The exchange of applications shall take place in electronic form within the EMCS.
The following acts are included in administrative cooperation between EU Member States: requests for administrative cooperation (request for verification, request for information on the management of excise duties, request for confirmation of registration in SEED); reply to a request for administrative cooperation; spontaneous information; an event report; control report.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
Authorisation and registration
In the Czech Republic, permanent tax supervision is applied to tax warehouses for alcohol, in the Czech Republic this supervision is replaced by continuous supervision of the tax administrator through a tracking device.
In the Czech Republic, small independent breweries are a tax warehouse, in the Czech Republic they are only registered by the tax administrator.
In The Czech Republic there is an institute of registered sender, which is included in the Tax Warehouse in the Czech Republic.
In the SR, it is possible to burn 43 l a with a reduced rate of excise duty on alcohol in the case of cultivation burning.
On the other hand, in the Czech Republic, the reduced rate of alcohol tax can only be applied to 30 l a.
The distillery in the Czech Republic must be authorised not only from the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Development of the Czech Republic, but also from the tax administrator.
In the Czech Republic, only the Ministry of Agriculture permits the distillery.
In The Czech National Court, the import of consumer packaging of alcohol is carried out in addition to the tax warehouse operator by the importer of consumer packaging of alcohol.
The authorisation of the importer shall be subject to registration by the applicant with the excise duty administrator.
In the Czech Republic, no special permission from the tax administrator is required to import consumer packaging of alcohol.
In SR, the sale of consumer packaging of alcohol is subject to the issue of a tax administrator's permit for sellers.
The seller of consumer packaging of alcohol has a legal obligation to keep records, inter alia, of the product concerned. purchase and sale.
In the Czech Republic, the tax administrator does not issue any permit for the final seller of consumer packaging of alcohol, it is sufficient to issue a concession for the sale of alcohol by the trade authority; the final seller does not keep any special records.
In SR, the seller of the fuel must have permission from the tax administrator to sell them.
The national legislation in the Slovak Technical Union does not regulate any special regulation of the pumping station, all activities related to filling stations are regulated only in the Law on excise duty on mineral oils.
In the Czech Republic, petrol stations are regulated by a special fuel law, but the tax administrator does not issue any permits for the sale of fuel.
Petrol stations are registered and their list is published by the Ministry of Industry and Trade.
In SR, it is not technically possible to obtain a list of petrol stations from the financial management system.
Since 2012, there has been a significant increase in the number of selected permits or registrations of tax entities in the Czech Technical Region.
This increase was due to a legislative change in that period.
In the Czech Republic, on the other hand, the number of selected permits decreased significantly in 2013 due to the introduction of a deposit for fuel distributors.
Administrative tasks
In the Czech Technical Court, substantive legislation provides for the obligation to exercise tax control for selected tax entities.
This issue is further specified by the internal management act issued by the FŘ SR due to the application of a single procedure of tax administrations in the territory of the SR.
In the Czech Republic, the substantive legislation does not regulate the obligation to carry out tax control, the procedural law provides only for the possibility of carrying out an inspection no later than the time limit for the assessment of the tax.
The reason for the large differences in the number of tax checks carried out and local investigations in the Slovak Republic and the Czech Republic is that the internal management act of the FŘ SR determines in which cases and within what time limits the tax administrator must carry out a tax audit, whereas in the Czech Republic the correctness of the amount of excise duty granted or its refund is verified mainly by local investigation.
The number of comparable administrative tasks in the Czech Republic has increased since 2012 due to an increase in the number of services in the EMCS system and at the same time as a result of an increase in the number of tax returns submitted.
In the SR, the number of administrative tasks between 2012 and 2015 had a slightly increasing trend, which was influenced by the increasing number of transports in the EMCS system and at the same time the decrease in the number of tax returns.
Evaluation
There were differences between the number of comparable permits and the registration of tax entities.
The number of comparable administrative tasks of tax administrations was similar in the Czech Republic in the individual years of the period audited.
In the Czech Republic, the total number of comparable tax entities, which is approximately two-thirds compared to the number of tax entities in the Czech Republic, accounts for approximately the same number of administrative tasks.
It can be stated from this that the SR is more focused on carrying out administrative tasks to the tax authorities, e.g. the tax authorities. physical tax surveillance.
In the Czech Republic, the emphasis is more on remote supervision, e.g. in the czech republic. tracking device, the immediate sending of data via the web interface and risk analysis.
Electronization of administrative tasks
Electronization of administrative tasks in the Czech Republic
The tax return can be filed via the data box.
The Customs Administration of the Czech Republic has introduced a so-called interactive tax return forms, which can no longer be processed in an automated manner.
The data must also be rewritten into the personal tax account of the tax entity.
The benefit is to limit the error rate of filed tax returns (DAP), which savings the tax administrator's actions related to the repair procedure erroneously filed by DAP.
DGC is working on a new dap electronic processing application.
Furthermore, by means of smart forms: to submit tax applications or registrations for activity and to notify of changes in data, to make refunds, to fulfil notification obligations in the treatment of special mineral oils, to the management of raw tobacco and to fulfil biofuel obligations.
The handling of control tapes is recorded by tax entities in the ORO WebClient information system, which is available to registered entities for registration by the tax administrator of the specified data.
Transport of selected products around the Czech Republic under the conditional exemption procedure must be carried out in the Czech Republic on the basis of an electronic accompanying document, which is implemented in the Czech Republic as a national functionality into the electronic system for monitoring the transport of selected products (EMCS).
The transport of selected products in free tax circulation in the tax territory of the Czech Republic can always be carried out with a document proving their taxation, proof of exemption from excise duty, decision of the customs office on the placing of the selected products under the customs procedure, a simplified accompanying document or any other decision on the assessment of excise duty.
The required content of the data is determined by law.
To facilitate the fulfilment of these obligations, the Czech Republic has introduced a voluntary electronic system for issuing alternative documents (Section 5 and Section 6 of Act No. 353/2003 Coll.).
This allows the paper form of documents to be replaced or supplemented by electronically issued documents, which are sent via the web interface of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic to the data warehouse, where each such document is assigned a unique 12-digit identification code (JIK).
The JIK serves for the purposes of customs control on the way and prevents repeated transport on the same document.
For the largest operator of the tax fuel warehouse in the Czech Republic, which puts about half of the volume of PHM into free tax circulation, CS ČR has online access to an electronic registration system into which the entity automatically stores issued tax documents.
CS Cr is considering the introduction of e-VDO, i.e. electronic system for the registration and monitoring of the transport of selected products carried out in free tax circulation.
This system should benefit from 70 % of the existing EMCS functional specification.
The advantage will be a user-known environment for declarants and customs officers.
It will also be linked to the global guarantee system, to the tax entity register or to the risk analysis system.
The system should allow for an overview of free circulation between Member States, which so far operates on the basis of written documents without registration and the sharing of the negotiating numbers by means of simplified accompanying documents.
The risks of the current process of recording the transport of selected products in free circulation can be seen mainly in the misuse of a simplified accompanying document, the re-use of a single document or illegal transport without any document.
Electronization of administrative tasks in SR
In the administration of excise duties, the Financial Administration of the SR uses electronic communication in monitoring the movement of goods in the EMCS system under the conditional exemption regime, stamp marks, the filing of tax returns, as well as the registration and registration of tax entities.
In 2014, one-way electronic communication between tax entities with the tax administrator was also introduced, which was extended to two-way communication in 2016.
In the context of electronic communication, the tax entity has a personal internet zone, the so-called "internet zone", made available after entering the access data. electronic personal mailbox, which is intended for communication with financial management.
Within this zone, the tax entity has access to the electronic mail room through which it submits applications, notifications, tax returns and other documents relating to the administration of excise duties.
However, electronic communication through a personal internet zone does not apply to all tax entities.
National legislation defines tax entities that are obliged to communicate with the tax administrator electronically.
These are primarily value added tax payers, tax advisors representing the tax entity and lawyers representing the tax entity.
The SAO SR also addressed the issue of the extent of electronisation of excise tax administration during the inspection.
These were only fully electronic acts, namely tax returns and electronic communications within ELO.
If the transports carried out in the EMCS system are taken away, there has been an increase in the electronisation of selected comparable administrative tasks, which is also a requirement for modern tax administration.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
Fully electronized processing of the tax return is already in place in the Czech Court, from its filing to the registration of the tax liability.
In the Czech Republic, electronic processing of tax return is not set up.
In the Czech Republic, the possibility for tax entities is set up to insert mandatory documents for individual transports in free tax circulation on the website.
In the future, the reporting of transport in free tax circulation in the form and basis of the EMCS system is being prepared.
Evaluation
The system of reporting services in free tax circulation in the Czech Republic contributes to tax supervision, thus eliminating the transport of selected products for which, contrary to the legislation, excise duty has not been paid.
These can be recommended as good practice.

Analysis of changes in organizational structure and personnel security in the field of excise duties
The organisation of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic and the Financial Administration of the Czech Republic have undergone major changes.
Organization of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic
Customs administration of the Czech Republic from 1. 1. 2013 consists of the Directorate-General of Customs and Customs Offices, which are administrative offices and departments of the State.
DGC is an entity for the entire customs administration.
Since 2004, the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic has been carrying out a comprehensive administration of excise duties as one of the many competences it provides.
CS CR also performs:
(a) control:
In the field of road transport (weighing of trucks, payment of charges for the use of roads, fulfilment of conditions for the carriage of dangerous goods, professional supervision of the work of crews of vehicles in international road freight transport and in matters of international transport of persons),
The management of waste and packaging material,
The safety of imported food,
in the field of consumer protection and the protection of intellectual property rights,
The employment of foreigners,
b) customs administration – it is a comprehensive application of customs legislation, commercial policy measures and formalities in the import and export of goods,
(c) the collection and recovery of pecuniary transactions imposed by other public authorities within the framework of a divided administration;
d) the activities of the police authority (authorized customs authorities) in the proceedings on crimes committed by customs and related regulations and tax regulations, if the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic is the tax administrator.
Although the scope of competences (the confluence of control activities) increases the overall cost of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic, there are cost savings from the scope, since the public administration does not have to spend on the status of the control group for each subject of the inspection separately.
At the same time, the administrative burden on the persons inspected is reduced by repeated checks.
10 The Customs Administration of the Czech Republic also carries out, from 1 January 2005, the customs authorities of the Czech Republic on the implementation of the 12. 2016 scope for the examination of the fulfilment of obligations in the registration of sales (Section 2(2) of Act No. 112/2016 Coll., on the registration of sales) and from 1. 1. 2017 supervision of compliance with the law and the conditions of the operation of gambling, including the imposition of penalties (Section 116 of Act No. 186/2016 Coll., on Gambling).
As part of the project Modernization of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic, the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic has changed with effect from 1 January 2009. 1. 2013 a three-stage structure on a two-stage basis, with the abolition of the central article of the procedure (customs directorates).
DGC spent around EUR 51 million on the project. (i.e. about €2,031,000).
CS CR from 1. 1. 2013 consists of DGC and regional customs offices, which are administrative offices and departments of the State.
Customs offices and their competences provided by law, the administration of excise duties is carried out by all customs offices through departments and territorial workplaces.
Territorial workplaces are internal organizational units of customs offices.
The Ministry of Finance is entitled to establish and abolish the territorial workplace and to determine their substantive scope.
The legislation does not provide for any competences for the territorial workplace; the competences of the customs office on its behalf.

As a result of the reorganisation of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic, there was no savings in personnel resources.
The performance of the main processes is carried out by customs officers in the service under the Law on the service of members of the security forces.
The possibility of reducing the number of these officers is very limited in the Czech Republic, since according to the provisions of § 42 para. 1 of Act No. 361/2003 Coll., on the service of members of the security forces, may be dismissed from the service only in cases exhaustively defined.
The reduction of posts due to organisational changes in the security corps is not a reason for dismissal and the employer is obliged to provide the staff with the assignment of appropriate posts within the Corps, or to provide posts with another security body (e.g. Police of the Czech Republic, Prison Service of the Czech Republic), otherwise they will be transferred to a reserve for the temporarily unclassified, in which members of the security forces belong according to the law 80 % of the average service income.

Organisation of excise tax administration in The Czech Technical Society
In the framework of the 2012-2016 programme statement, the Government of the Slovak Republic has identified as one of the priorities the completion of tax administration reform through the UNITAS programme, which will provide additional budgetary resources by unifying the collection of taxes, customs duties and levies and the suppression of tax evasion.
In this context, tax reform was implemented at the central level, which brought about the merger of the Tax Directorate of the Czech National System of the Czech National System and the Customs Directorate of the Czech National System into the Financial Directorate of the Czech System of The Czech System and the creation of financial administration.
The SR F.C. was established on 1 January 2004. 1. 2012 by Act No. 333/2011 Z. z., on state administration bodies in the field of taxation, fees and customs, as amended, as a budgetary organisation, which has its seat in Banská Bystrica and is connected to the state budget through the budget chapter of the Ministry of Finance of the Slovak Republic.
FŘ SR, CÚ and the Criminal Office of The Financial Administration within the meaning of Act No. 199/2004 Z. z., the Customs Act and on the amendment and addition of certain laws, as amended, are the customs authorities if they perform tasks under customs legislation.
Within the meaning of Act No. 333/2011 Z. z., on state administration bodies in the field of taxation, fees and customs, as amended, together with the tax authorities form the financial administration.
The new organisational structure of the financial administration as at 1 January 2005 is not the case. The main mission of the FŘ SR is to collect and manage taxes and customs duties efficiently, i.e. to collect taxes and customs duties. consumption taxes, to meet the revenue portion of the state budget and to protect the economic interests of the state.
The statutory body of the FŘ SR is the President of the Financial Administration, appointed and dismissed by the Minister of Finance of the Slovak Republic.
